\DoxyCodeLine{00083\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Color-\/Order:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00084\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ specified\ order\ of\ color\ components\ red,\ green\ and\ blue\ affects\ 24-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00085\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ 32-\/bit\ images\ of\ type\ FIT\_BITMAP\ as\ well\ as\ the\ colors\ that\ are\ part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00086\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ of\ a\ color\ palette.\ All\ other\ images\ always\ use\ RGB\ order.\ By\ default,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00087\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ color\ order\ is\ coupled\ to\ endianness:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00088\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ little-\/endian\ -\/>\ BGR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00089\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ big-\/endian\ \ \ \ -\/>\ RGB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00090\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ However,\ you\ can\ always\ define\ FREEIMAGE\_COLORORDER\ to\ any\ of\ the\ known}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00091\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ orders\ FREEIMAGE\_COLORORDER\_BGR\ (0)\ and\ FREEIMAGE\_COLORORDER\_RGB\ (1)\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00092\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ specify\ your\ preferred\ color\ order.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00093\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ FREEIMAGE\_COLORORDER\_BGR\ \ \ \ 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00094\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ FREEIMAGE\_COLORORDER\_RGB\ \ \ \ 1}}
